print:break-inside-avoid min-h-lh [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start self-start justify-start">index是为了根据基因组的位置对bam文件中mapping到相应位置的alignment records进行快速访问而设计出的一种数据结构。它大致可以理解成基因组上的位置与磁盘相应alignment records所在的chunk对应的offset之间的一个look up table。所以只有当bam文件根据coordinates排序后，才能利用<code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">samtools index</code>建立这种index。index文件通常有一个<code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))] break-words hyphens-none">.bai</code>后缀。</p></div></li></ul><!--$?--><template id="B:16"></template><!--/$--><h3 id="id-3.4-flagstat" class="text-lg @xs:text-xl @lg:text-2xl font-semibold heading pdf-heading flex </span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content"># flag 4 indicates unmapped<!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content">samtools view -bF 4  SRR1573434.sampled.bam &gt;  SRR1573434.sampled.F.4.bam<!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content">
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content"># extract unmapped reads<!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content">samtools view -bf 4  SRR1573434.sampled.bam &gt;  SRR1573434.sampled.f.4.bam<!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content">
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content"># discard reads pairs with unmapped read<!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content"># flag 4 indicates unmapped, flag 8 indicates mate unmapped<!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content"># flag 4+8=12 indicates read itself is unmapped or has unmapped mate <!-- -->
</span></span><span class="highlight-line"><span class="highlight-line-content">samtools view -bF 12 SRR1573434.sampled.bam &gt; SRR1573434.sampled.F.12.bam<!-- -->
